# ============================================================================
# CHAOS REDUX - EVENT 005 SOVIET COLLAPSE DECISIONS
# ============================================================================
# Opening Soviet goal-style objectives are hidden from normal purchase flow and
# activated by scripted effects with a ten-active-objective cap.
# ============================================================================

@soviet_collapse_mission_days_local_quick = 95
@soviet_collapse_mission_days_local_admin = 105
@soviet_collapse_mission_days_local_extended = 110
@soviet_collapse_mission_days_short_operational = 120
@soviet_collapse_mission_days_regional_operation = 150
@soviet_collapse_mission_days_rail_corridor = 165
@soviet_collapse_mission_days_republic_legitimacy = 180
@soviet_collapse_mission_days_foreign_pressure = 210
@soviet_collapse_mission_days_league_operation = 240
@soviet_collapse_mission_days_high_chaos_containment = 270
@soviet_collapse_mission_days_terminal_containment = 365
@soviet_collapse_response_days_reenable = 28
@soviet_collapse_breakaway_action_days_reenable = 35
@soviet_collapse_foreign_intervention_days_reenable = 45
@soviet_collapse_factory_ancient_days_reenable = 42
@soviet_collapse_ai_low = 1
@soviet_collapse_ai_medium = 2
@soviet_collapse_ai_high = 3
@soviet_collapse_ai_calm_multiplier = 0.5
@soviet_collapse_ai_pressure_multiplier = 2
@soviet_collapse_ai_urgent_multiplier = 3

soviet_collapse_soviet_category = {
	soviet_collapse_restore_party_control = {
		icon = GFX_decision_restore_party_control
		available = { can_pay_soviet_collapse_restore_party_control_cost = yes }
		visible = { tag = SOV is_soviet_collapse_active = yes }
		custom_cost_trigger = { can_pay_soviet_collapse_restore_party_control_cost = yes }
		custom_cost_text = soviet_collapse_restore_party_control_cost_text
		days_re_enable = @soviet_collapse_response_days_reenable
		complete_effect = {
			add_manpower = constant:soviet_collapse_decision_cost.restore_party_control_manpower_spend
			add_equipment_to_stockpile = { type = infantry_equipment amount = constant:soviet_collapse_decision_cost.restore_party_control_infantry_equipment_spend }
			add_equipment_to_stockpile = { type = support_equipment_1 amount = constant:soviet_collapse_decision_cost.restore_party_control_support_equipment_spend }
			add_to_variable = { soviet_collapse_moscow_authority = 5 }
			add_to_variable = { soviet_collapse_military_obedience = 2 }
			add_to_variable = { soviet_collapse_republic_confidence = -3 }
			add_ideas = soviet_collapse_emergency_union_authority
			soviet_collapse_recalculate_total_threat = yes
			custom_effect_tooltip = soviet_collapse_restore_party_control_tt
		}
		ai_will_do = {
			base = @soviet_collapse_ai_medium
			modifier = {
				factor = @soviet_collapse_ai_urgent_multiplier
				check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_moscow_authority value = constant:soviet_collapse_super_event.union_unmade_contested_authority compare = less_than }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = @soviet_collapse_ai_pressure_multiplier
				check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_total_collapse_threat value = constant:soviet_collapse_super_event.union_unmade_high_threat compare = greater_than }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = @soviet_collapse_ai_calm_multiplier
				check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_moscow_authority value = constant:soviet_collapse_baseline.moscow_authority compare = greater_than_or_equals }
			}
		}
	}
